Northeastern Tears and Dire Straits 93

Jehol Under Strain... Tang Yulin's Involvement is Significant

Yu Pass on the Brink... He Zhuguo's Lone Stand

Volunteer Army Exhausted... Eagerly Awaiting Assistance from All Sides

Tianjin Correspondence - The iron hooves of the Japanese army have already trampled all over the three eastern provinces. Eight customs checkpoints have been occupied and are now separated from the Nanjing General Customs Administration. The postal services of the three provinces are also scheduled to become independent on August 1st. The territory and sovereignty of the three provinces under the rule of the Republic of China are lost, completely lost! However, the Japanese have not yet fully satisfied their desires in losing the three eastern provinces. For nearly twenty years, they have been advocating a unified policy for Manchuria and Mongolia, and they are now carrying it out. Jehol, Beiping, Tianjin, and Chahar are all within their plan of gradual encroachment. They must acquire Jehol, Chahar, Beiping, and Tianjin before they can unite with Mongolia. Recently, the Japanese army has gradually concentrated in Yixian, and the police in Shanhaiguan frequently report alarms. Tang Yulin's attitude is particularly noteworthy. Tang has two representatives, one stationed in Shenyang and one in Changchun. Tang's property in Shenyang has suffered no losses, and Tang's name was also listed at the beginning of the puppet state's organization. Tang has not made any firm statements of rejection. Although Tang has stated that his difficult position forces him to feign compliance with the Japanese, if the Japanese army advances towards Jehol, then Tang must firmly express his attitude and can no longer be ambiguous. Whether he resolutely rises up to resist or follows in the footsteps of the Northeast Army by making an unresisting retreat is of great importance. His attitude is truly worthy of attention. He Zhuguo is indeed a hero. He wants to splatter the first pass under heaven, Yu Pass, with his hot blood, but unfortunately, the situation is no longer favorable for a lone stand. As long as the Japanese army advances on Yu Pass, it will eventually be difficult to defend because Zhang Xueliang has not paid attention to Yu Pass and made arrangements for a last-ditch defense.

Since the September 18th Incident, the people of the Northeast, fearing the pain of national and family destruction, have seen volunteer armies spring up everywhere, giving the Japanese army considerable punishment. If someone were to lead them, there would indeed be great prospects. The volunteer army's original intention of taking up arms to defend against the enemy clearly knew that their strength was limited and could not last, but they truly hoped that those responsible within the passes and the people of all provinces would provide tangible assistance. Unexpectedly, the months of January, February, March, April, May, and June have flown by like an arrow, and assistance has never materialized, causing those who sacrificed their lives for the country to be exposed in the sand without anyone caring, and those who were injured for the country to groan in the wilderness without anyone treating them. During the Battle of Shanghai, donations from various places to comfort the 19th Route Army were numerous, but there was very little comfort for the volunteer army outside the passes, causing the patriotic heroes to go from hope to disappointment and discouragement. Those who later raised the banner of the volunteer army,

A portion are bandits. Among the bandits, there are bound to be those who falsely use the name of volunteer armies to disturb the local area and hope for future recruitment. The Japanese are keenly aware of this situation and have recently formulated a plan to cut off the water at the source. Soon, they will start to appease the bandits and incorporate them into the puppet Manchukuo's national defense forces. These people are forced by hunger and cold, and we cannot blame them for surrendering to the enemy. The Japanese plan is to wait until all the appeasement is completed, then send Japanese officers to carry out military training, using various methods to numb their conscience, hoping to complete the training in three months. Then, they will drive them into the passes to have Chinese fight Chinese. If they win, they will open up territory for the puppet state; if they lose, the Japanese army will cut off their return route, and they will all die within the passes. Their plan is truly poisonous. As for the Black Army and the Self-Defense Forces, composed of local militias, led by Ma Zhanshan, Ding Chao, Li Du, etc., near the Middle East Railway, they are still fighting hard, but I am afraid that the day of exhaustion, depleted ammunition, and depleted food is not far off.

The magistrates and public security chiefs of the counties under the jurisdiction of the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang are mostly the same people as before the September 18th Incident. However, the county government dispatches one Japanese person to serve as an instructor, who controls everything and plays with the county magistrate at will. Among the county magistrates of the three provinces, there are many intelligent and patriotic individuals. After the incident, they could have brought their seals into the passes, but most of them valued their responsibility to defend the territory and dared not leave without authorization. They also hoped to recover the lost territory in a short period of time. Later, they realized that their hopes had become illusions and were controlled by the Japanese (instructors), becoming virtual prisoners from the beginning. Even if they wanted to break free, it was no longer possible. From the top of the puppet Manchukuo government down to the bureau chiefs and county magistrates, all have become puppets, manipulated by the Japanese. As for the people, they are eking out a living under the iron hooves. Whenever the Japanese encounter our compatriots, they ask, "What country are you from?" They must answer, "Manchukuo." Then they ask, "Is China good, or is Manchukuo good?" They must answer, "Manchukuo is good." If they answer that they are Chinese and that China is good, they will be beaten severely, even to death. Their lives are truly like mayflies. What is most concerning is that the general education of children has also been completely Japanized, numbing their minds and obliterating their conscience. When they grow up, they will only know Manchuria and Japan and will no longer know the Republic of China.

Mr. Zhu Zhaiqing has recently been in Beijing and Shanghai, encouraging the people to use force to recover the Northeast in order to fulfill their responsibility as citizens. We express our utmost sympathy. At present, the volunteer army, self-defense forces, national salvation army, and the armies of Ma Zhanshan, Ding Chao, and Li Du in the Northeast are about to be exhausted, but as long as there is supply and leadership, taking advantage of the time when the green gauze is rising, it is the best opportunity to recover the Northeast. We sincerely hope that Mr. Zhu can raise ammunition and military pay and save the 30 million people of the Northeast as soon as possible, and should not delay any longer. Because the Japanese's fundamental method for eliminating hidden dangers for the puppet Manchukuo, the first step is to incorporate the volunteer army, and the second step is to wait until the end of autumn to implement the clearing of the countryside under the pretext of winter defense. All civilian self-defense firearms must be reported and stamped; otherwise, if they are found, they will be charged with concealing military equipment and communicating with bandits. After the firearms owned by the people of the three provinces have been surveyed, the people will be ordered to carry their weapons to the nearest managing agency to request registration, inspection, and branding. The various rural clearing agencies will take this opportunity to confiscate the firearms. From then on, the 30 million people of the Northeast will become meat on the chopping block, to be slaughtered by foreign races.

In addition, there is also an event that is part of the Japanese conspiracy to occupy the three eastern provinces. In 1930, the "Manzhou Daily" published the "Biographies of Northeast Figures," extensively advertising in the newspaper to solicit information about the deeds, properties, and addresses of Northeast figures, seeking as much detail as possible. Excluding first-class figures who were well-known to the Japanese and did not need to be solicited, roles of the second and third class or lower would either submit articles themselves or hire someone to write them. They would exaggerate their own deeds and faithfully write about their properties to show their wealth. It is said that the newspaper spent no less than 200,000 yuan on soliciting articles, printing, and other expenses. Over 4,000 people were listed in the "Biographies of Northeast Figures," a truly impressive sight. Recently, if the puppet Manchukuo wants to confiscate the properties of Northeast figures, it does not need to conduct investigations; it can simply browse through the "Biographies of Northeast Figures" and find them according to the map without missing a single one. However, the implementation of this matter is still under consideration because the properties of many important people are insured by various powerful countries. If they are confiscated rashly, it will inevitably lead to many negotiations. However, this is only a matter of time. With the cunning of the Japanese, they will eventually find a way to deal with it. (July 16th)

Deterioration Between Japan and Russia 94

Japanese Police Arriving in Manchuria Opposed by Russia

Russia Sends Red Army to Increase Stationing on the Border to Demonstrate

The Incident at the Jiangbin Wharf Has Become Serious

Manzhouli Correspondence - In the past week, the relationship between Japan and Russia has become increasingly tense. Soviet Russia has also changed from being weak and soft to being strong and tough.

One hundred and sixty Japanese international police officers arrived in Manzhouli a month ago. Initially, they planned to begin service immediately, but the Soviet Russian consul raised questions, saying that Manzhouli belongs to the Sino-Russian border area. If the Japanese police came here to protect overseas Chinese, then they should not have local police power. Soviet Russia also has a number of overseas Chinese here. If Japan publicly implements police administration, Soviet Russia should also allocate Red Army troops to come to cooperate. Therefore, the Japanese side did not dare to serve as police officers in the city. This is a past matter. On the 12th of this month, the Red Army on the Soviet Russian border suddenly increased by many. More than 3,000 infantry and artillery troops were moved over to the No. 86 border station, approaching Manzhouli. On the morning of the 13th, more than 80 artillery shells were fired at both Datori and Abagaitu, and aircraft also soared into the air and circled before stopping in Manzhouli in the afternoon. Although the Japanese consul knew that the intention was to demonstrate, he did not dare to ask. Two Soviet Russian shallow-water warships outside Sanjiangkou sailed to and crossed Tongjiang to reach near Fujin a few days ago. Japanese aircraft urgently scouted, but the Russian warships were ingeniously equipped, with very little exposed above the water surface. Flying at low altitude was feared due to anti-aircraft artillery fire, so they ultimately failed to ascertain the situation and returned. In recent days, artillery fire and the sound of aircraft dropping bombs have been heard in Hulin, Xu Ergu, and Molihong, causing border residents to panic and move inland one after another. There are many Chinese soldiers along the border who have crossed the river to Soviet Russian territory or have been recruited to go there. There is a training center in both Bolik and Chita that specializes in training Chinese soldiers. Japanese spies reported to their military headquarters that they had confirmed that there were 1,700 people being trained in Bolik and 2,000 in Chita. They will be used against the Japanese army in Manchuria and as guides for the Red Army. A few days ago, a train arrived at the Hailin station on the Harbin-Suifenhe Railway, carrying 1,000 international communist soldiers. They planned to attack Shitouhezi, but they retreated because the Japanese army was prepared. This proves that the two incidents of Soviet Russia training communist soldiers in Bolik and Chita, which the Japanese side detected, are not fictitious. In Harbin, Soviet Russian important figures have recently been secretly returning to their country. Only the Consul General Shiratori and the Board Director Danilevsky and Deputy Board Director Kuznetszov remain. Because the manager of the Faya Bank, Mesherny, arrived in Harbin to discuss purchasing the Middle East Railway with the Japanese, he has been waiting in Harbin for many days. Now, on the 12th, he suddenly ordered his secretary to send his wife and children back to the country first, and he himself, accompanied by Deputy Consul Lasheman, took a train back to Moscow on the 13th. When passing through Manzhouli, he inspected the Manzhouli Customs. Because the Manzhouli branch of the customs is close to the Russian border and the Sino-Russian trade agreement has not been finalized, Soviet Russian goods are constantly arriving. China and Russia had signed a land tax collection agreement, and there are also Soviet Russian customs officials. The relationship with Soviet Russia is therefore extremely close. After the Northeast was forcibly occupied by Japan, Soviet Russia regarded it as a terminal point for pushing goods, which has been cut off, causing displeasure. This time, the Japanese side again made the puppet state forcibly collect taxes from various customs offices without consulting Russia before or after the fact, making Russia even more displeased. Previously, Soviet Russia was in a period of tolerance and did not ask about anything. Now, the attitude of Soviet Russia has changed to be strong. In this matter, they will not let go. If Kuznetszov's inspection reveals any unfavorable aspects to Soviet Russia, it may lead to a serious situation. It is also heard that Mr. Ku returned to the country to report on the situation within Manchuria, saying that Soviet Russia recalled various important figures to express its determination to Japan. This can be seen from the fact that the puppet state forcibly took over the Jiangbin Middle East Railway cargo warehouse, which has become a major issue. The Middle East Railway originally leased a section of land at Jiangbin Station from the Jiangyun Office to build the Jiangbin Wharf and Commercial Agency, with the aim of facilitating water and land transportation. It has been leasing for many years, and the contract has been renewed every year, with the rent being 15,000 rubles. This year, the puppet state, created by Japan, refused to renew the contract and did not pay the rent. Therefore, Japan manipulated the puppet Jiangyun Office to forcibly take it back and operate it themselves on the 8th, citing the non-performance of the contract and the non-payment of rent as reasons. After this incident occurred, Japan thought that Soviet Russia has always been weak and that it would likely have no recourse. Who knew that the Russian side would completely change its past demeanor? In addition to the Middle East Railway Board Director requesting the puppet governor to convene a meeting to resolve the matter, at the same time, Consul General Shiratori also lodged a serious protest and visited the puppet Ministry of Foreign Affairs twice to question the Japanese, Sugihara, the director of the puppet General Affairs Office. On the 11th, he also sent a strongly worded written

Page 9

Summary of Important News 95

protest, saying that the Middle East Railway property belongs to Imperial Russia. Soviet Russia inherited the rights of the Middle East Railway based on the Sino-Russian and Fengtian-Russian agreements. Everything of the Middle East Railway belongs to Russia. Although China and Russia are nominally co-managed, it is only a nominal distinction. Whether the Manchukuo has the right to enjoy the Middle East Railway business on behalf of China is still in question. The Jiangbin Wharf is Middle East Railway land, and its internal land cannot be taken over. Sugihara, because the case was important, went to Changchun to meet the puppet Vice Minister, the Japanese Ohashi Tadashi, and returned to Harbin on the 13th. Because he had not received orders from the Japanese side, he did not dare to attend. Heilongjiang Volunteer Army Greatly Defeats Japanese Army 96

Killed More Than 400 Japanese Soldiers in Gaolingzi

Inflicted Numerous Deaths and Injuries on Japanese Soldiers in Laha City

Hailun Correspondence - On July 12th, the National Salvation Army under Wang Delin captured Daohezi, a station on the Harbin-Suifenhe Railway. The Japanese army had dispatched a large force from Mianpo to counterattack. It is reported that at 5 p.m. that afternoon, the Japanese army under the Itaya Brigade, totaling approximately 3,000 troops, boarded a train and headed towards Yinma River. However, upon reaching Gaolingzi, because the mountain terrain was treacherous and the railway track was built on the ridge, the vehicles had to pass through a winding path, making the journey very tortuous. The National Salvation Army had 미리 prepared three freight cars at the highest winding path and dismantled the winding path at the foot of the mountain. When the Japanese train approached and was blocked at the foot of the mountain, the National Salvation Army dismantled the track on the side of the mountain peak, causing the three freight cars to roll down the mountain slope and fall to the foot of the mountain, directly smashing into the Japanese train. Seven of the cars were immediately pulverized, and the remaining cars also overturned beside the railway track. Gunpowder inside a railway car

Was detonated, creating a huge explosion. Approximately 400 soldiers and officers were reduced to powder, and countless pieces of equipment and wheels were damaged. There were also many light and serious injuries. By the morning of the 13th, the Japanese army from Mianpo had arrived to provide assistance and transported the wounded and dead back to Hengdaohezi. The area east of Hengdaohezi was then in the hands of the National Salvation Army. The news of this event spread to various places, and everyone who heard it was overjoyed. On the same day this event occurred, a fierce battle also broke out on the banks of the Nen River in Heilongjiang. The Heilongjiang army under Xu Zihe and Xu Baozhen killed hundreds of Japanese soldiers. The cause was that the Japanese army in Nehe had pressured the Heilongjiang army under Xu Baozhen to withdraw from the city on the 10th. Afterwards, the Japanese armies in Nehe, Laha, and Nenjiang, totaling more than 5,000 troops, had formed a line to block the Heilongjiang army's path to attack Heilongjiang. The Japanese army guarding Nehe was the Koizumi Regiment, consisting of 2,500 infantry and 500 artillery. The Japanese army guarding Nenjiang was the Owari River Cavalry Regiment, consisting of approximately 1,700 troops. The Japanese army guarding Laha Station was the Toiya Infantry Company, along with artillery and cavalry, totaling 500 troops. On the 10th, the Japanese army was digging trenches at these three locations, planning to build deep ditches and high fortifications to trap the Heilongjiang army. Also, the main force of the Hiramatsu Brigade launched an attack on the volunteer army led by Cai Hongyou in Keshan, so they did not pressure the Heilongjiang army near Nenjiang. On the 12th, the armies of Xu Baozhen and Xu Zihe launched a siege on Laha Station, the central point of the Japanese army on the banks of the Nen River, and divided their forces to defend against the reinforcements of the Owari River and Koizumi near the banks of the Nen River and Nehe. At 8 p.m. that afternoon, when it was dark and the Japanese aircraft could not take off, they took the opportunity to launch a fierce attack. The Japanese army was besieged in Laha City, and could not escape left or right. More than 100 Japanese residents also joined the battle, but the Heilongjiang army was exceptionally brave. Knowing that the Japanese army's aim was inaccurate in the dark, they used a strong force to charge forward and shout, chasing and killing the Japanese soldiers who had no way to escape. At approximately 2 a.m. on the morning of the 13th, the company commander Toiya and the infantry lieutenant Murano, along with four other officers, were killed by the broadsword team. Countless Japanese soldiers were killed by artillery fire and broadswords. The remaining forces protected the Japanese residents and retreated towards the Qiqihar Road, which is the same road. The Heilongjiang army entered Laha City at 3 a.m. on the 13th. This place is a dangerous strategic point in northeastern Heilongjiang and also an important road to attack the provincial capital from northern Heilongjiang. After entering the city, the Heilongjiang army stationed troops inside and outside to guard it. During the fierce battle, a Japanese resident of Laha, Takai, escaped to the Ningnian station on the Qiqihar Road and telegraphed Nenjiang and Nehe for help. The Owari River Cavalry mobilized all their troops to rescue them, but upon reaching the banks of the Nen River, there was no bridge to cross due to the late hour, and it had also been burned by the Heilongjiang army. They then traveled quickly along the river, but were intercepted by the Heilongjiang army. Countless people drowned in the water. The remaining forces retreated to the Ningnian station. The Heilongjiang army immediately surrounded them outside the station. They were still in confrontation on the 13th. The Japanese army had lost their supplies for a day and night and were on the verge of being resolved by the Heilongjiang army. After the Koizumi Infantry received the emergency report from Laha, they rushed to the vicinity of Laha at 11 a.m. on the 13th, but were again fiercely attacked head-on by the Heilongjiang army and returned to Nehe to defend themselves. Upon receiving the report of the crisis in Laha, four Japanese aircraft flew to Laha and dropped more than ten bombs, but were repelled by the Heilongjiang army's artillery fire. According to the reconnaissance report from the aircraft, the Heilongjiang army, numbering approximately 7,000 to 8,000, had dug trenches on the left bank of the Nen River to defend and intended to stay there for a long time. The Japanese army stationed in Heilongjiang had already advanced in that direction, and a brigade of the Japanese army stationed in Harbin also departed in that direction on the 13th. There will likely be a fierce battle in that area. (14th)

Discussing the Current Situation in Rehe with Tan Guohuan 97

Tang Yulin Determined to Defend Territory

Mongolian Bandits Disturbing Rehe Have Been Cleared

A recent dispatch from Beiping regarding the Rehe issue has varied reports. To clarify the current situation in Rehe, this reporter specifically visited Tan Guohuan, Secretary-General of the Rehe Provincial Government, to inquire about the military and administrative conditions in various parts of the province. Mr. Tan made the following statement:

(Since the September 18th Incident, Premier Tang (Yulin) of Rehe Province has recognized the extreme importance of the province's defense due to its proximity to the Northeast. He has therefore resolved to protect the land and ensure the people's safety, aligning himself with the central government's intentions. Regarding the Japanese residents within Rehe Province, fearing incidents, special troops were dispatched to provide strict protection at all times. In Chifeng, where a Japanese consulate was located, the Japanese Consul, Mr. Muta, consulted with the provincial government, and it was decided that all Japanese residents in Rehe would withdraw uniformly. The Japanese consul also reported the number of departing Japanese residents to the provincial government in detail. Chairman Tang dispatched guards to escort the Japanese residents out of the province, ensuring that all Japanese residents arrived safely in Beiping. Mr. Yano Makoto, acting charge d'affaires of the Japanese legation in Beiping, personally sent a letter to the Rehe Provincial Government expressing his gratitude for Rehe's protection of Japanese residents. At that time, the Rehe Provincial Government reported the entire situation to the central government and Director Zhang. After the Japanese residents left Rehe, the local area remained peaceful. Recently, Japan has been using Mongolian cavalry and bandits to create disturbances in Chaoyang East, Kailu, and Lingyuan. The eastern part of Chaoyang is mostly high mountains and valleys. When the Mongolian bandits caused disturbances, Rehe Province sent troops to attack, and fortunately, the Mongolian bandits were cleared within less than half a month. Although there have been various rumors about the recent situation in Rehe, Chief Secretary Tang (Zuo Fu) recently came to Beiping from Chengde, and the Chaoyang East incident was resolved long ago. The provincial government first sent Zhang Bingyi, Director of the Civil Affairs Department, to inspect and investigate the local situation in detail. After Director Zhang returned to the province, based on his report, Chairman Tang immediately dismissed all corrupt officials and reassigned Li Zhizhen as the magistrate of Chaoyang County and Zhang Lin as the commander of the local militia. Magistrate Li has a very harmonious relationship with the people. The county has a long-standing reputation for being difficult to govern, which proves that maintaining local security is not easy. The Yixian area on the border of Rehe is very close to Beizhen and Jinxi. The dangerous locations such as Hongluoxian, Da Yaogou, Nuan Ditang, and the mountainous areas of Kailu and Lingyuan in Rehe have natural barriers that are difficult to penetrate, and the small mountain paths are rugged and large vehicles cannot travel side by side, making transportation difficult. Other locations such as Lengkou and Xifengkou are also natural fortifications. Chairman Tang previously sent his second son to Beiping, and he has already reported to Director Zhang. Director Zhang and Chairman Tang are still exchanging telegrams, which proves that the rumors are not true. According to recent reports, there are four regiments of Japanese troops stationed in Yixian, coveting the situation in Rehe. According to reliable reports from Rehe yesterday, there have recently been refugees from Yixian arriving in Rehe. According to the refugees, the number of Japanese troops in Yixian is very small, with forty of them residing in the home of Director Li of the Rehe Construction Department, who is from Yixian. The Japanese troops in Yixian came from Beipiao. Although there have recently been Mongolian bandit activities, they have not significantly affected the security of Rehe. Although there are many doubts about Chairman Tang, such as the Gilin Daily publishing a copperplate map that includes Rehe as part of Manchuria and claiming that Tang has accepted various appointments, these actions are entirely for Japanese propaganda purposes. Although the Japanese have not forgotten their intentions towards Rehe, Chairman Tang, for the sake of the overall situation, is determined to defend the territory. Mr. Tai Bing-san (Xi-ling) personally visited Rehe in April this year to inspect the local situation, and he is very clear about the situation. Because I have been assigned to come to Beiping, the date of my return to Rehe is undetermined. Chief Secretary Tang went to Tianjin yesterday and will return to Chengde within a few days." (18th)

Chiang Kai-shek Bans Opium and Prostitution in Hankou 98

Orders Military and Police Agencies to Strictly Enforce

A dispatch from Hankou: Commander-in-Chief Chiang has come to Hankou to supervise the troops and suppress bandits, vigorously rectifying the military and eliminating decadent customs. Yesterday, the 18th, Chiang issued an order to strictly investigate and ban opium dens and brothels, with a deadline of the 23rd to completely eliminate them. On the 19th, he also ordered the Wuhan Garrison Headquarters and the Hankou Public Security Bureau to strictly suppress prostitution and stipulate provisional regulations. Military and government personnel who solicit prostitutes or stay in brothels will be immediately arrested. The order stated:

"It has been found that there are many prostitutes in the city of Hankou, and their decadent customs are deeply harmful to society. Therefore, this order requires the relevant departments to strictly suppress prostitution. Prostitutes in all large and small hotels in Hankou must move to brothels and are not allowed to linger in public places. The suppression must be completed before the 23rd of this month. If there are any more hotels where women engage in prostitution, or any public or private places that solicit prostitutes, once discovered, the relevant departments will be held accountable and will not be lenient. In addition to separate orders, this order is issued to ensure compliance and diligent execution."

Attached: Provisional Regulations for Suppressing Prostitution

(1) Any current military or government personnel found to have solicited prostitutes or stayed in brothels will be immediately arrested.

(2) If any military or government personnel enter a brothel, the brothel must report it to the military police for arrest, otherwise the brothel will be punished along with them.

(3) All public and private places are strictly prohibited from soliciting prostitutes.

(4) All brothels must display signs.

(5) All prostitutes must wear flowers to identify them.

(6) Private prostitutes will be strictly suppressed.

(7) Prostitutes in this city are not allowed to stay in large or small hotels and must all move into brothels.

(8) Prostitutes are strictly prohibited from soliciting customers in public places and streets.

(9) The Garrison Headquarters is responsible for ensuring compliance within the special third district.

(10) The Garrison Headquarters is responsible for enforcing the first two articles of these regulations. The Public Security Bureau is responsible for enforcing all other articles. (July 19th)

Faculty and Staff to Petition in Beijing En Masse

Yesterday, the fifth general meeting of the National Labor University Faculty and Staff School Protection Association was held. All faculty and staff, including Zhang Yuanzhe, Han Yanmen, and Li Ying, attended. Wang Cheng served as chairman, and Chen Zhen served as recorder. Two important resolutions were passed, as follows: (1) It was resolved to telegraph the Ministry of Education, welcoming the dispatch of personnel for takeover, but only after fulfilling two conditions: (1) Immediately formally announce the Labor University Revival Plan; (2) Fully pay all back wages. The original telegram text is recorded below: (To the esteemed Ministry of Education in Nanjing: We have heard that the Ministry is dispatching personnel to take over our school. Our colleagues have long awaited the handover with great joy. We hope that the back wages will be allocated at the same time to facilitate the closure. We also hope that the Ministry will consider the difficulty of establishing this school and the ardent expectations of the people of the whole country, and immediately announce the revival and reorganization plan to prevent this only labor education institution from being destroyed by Japanese artillery fire. Otherwise, we colleagues can only vow to fight to the end with our sincere school protection spirit. Respectfully, the National Labor University School Protection Committee.)

(2) It was resolved that faculty and staff will go to Beijing en masse within days to petition and demand back wages from the Ministry of Education, thereby urging the Ministry to pay attention to its duties and respect its responsibilities.

In addition, it is reported that Mr. Ma Xiangbo, the "Ninety-Three Old Man," could not bear to see Labor University destroyed by artillery fire from Japan and then suspended by the Ministry of Education. He repeatedly wrote to important figures in the Beijing government, requesting that they withdraw the order. This was reported earlier. It has now been learned that the old man recently wrote to Cai Yuanpei, the founder of Labor University, asking him to write to the Ministry of Education in the name of the Academia Sinica, requesting that it revoke the order to close Labor University. His original letter is as follows: (To Mr. Zimin: I recently heard that you returned to Shanghai from giving lectures in Wuhan. I think of your virtuous efforts in founding the National Labor University. Now, the Ministry of Education's division chiefs have ordered its closure because the school cannot easily raise funds after the January 28th Incident. However, you once traveled to Europe. After the European war, all universities that were destroyed did their best to rebuild, both to awaken the national spirit of common hatred and to show that national planning prioritizes culture. This closure order is insufficient to show to foreign countries and the people of the country. Moreover, labor is the foundation of people's livelihood. What I have heard and seen makes me feel compelled to speak to you. Would it be possible to write to the National Government's Ministry of Education in the name of the Academia Sinica, requesting that it revoke the order to close Labor University, leaving a glimmer of hope for the people and comforting the teachers and students of the school who are reducing expenses, maintaining hardship, and earnestly serving the country? Poor and needy children will also be able to receive higher vocational education. I don't know if this is appropriate for your wisdom. [The rest omitted])

Cai Jie Min Praises Best-Selling University and Middle School Entrance Examination Guides 108

A Precious Treasure for Young Students

A True Compass for Advancement and Entrance Examinations

The Qinfen Bookstore, located at No. M117, Huajinli Intersection, Four Horse Road, Shanghai, is responding to the current need for advancement and entrance examinations by issuing two major works: University Entrance Examination Guide and Middle School Entrance Examination Guide. The two series were compiled by 　Jieshao Ji, a famous educator with rich educational experience. Cai Jie Min wrote the title and praised them, saying that the collection is thorough and the description is clear, which can indeed be used as a guide for those who aspire to advance, and he is happy to introduce them. Each book is priced at six corners, and an additional postage fee is required for mail orders. The price is low and the quality is good, and the application is extremely large. The former book has a total of six chapters, and the latter book has a total of seven chapters. Each chapter is divided into sections, and according to the level and needs of universities and middle schools, everything about advancement, registration, entrance examinations, enrollment, course selection, and intellectual, physical, and economic conditions, as well as the current status of various universities and middle schools, is compiled in detail and provides practical guidance. They are truly a secret treasure for students and a compass for entrance examinations. Now is the summer vacation, and various schools are recruiting new students, so students from middle schools and above in this city and other places, as well as colleagues in the book industry, are directly writing to the bureau to purchase and wholesale them. Many school authorities have even purchased them in bulk to distribute to graduates so that they can use them as a reference for entrance examinations. However, it is heard that the bureau has a limited number of printed books and not much stock. Because sales are so strong and young people need them urgently, they have already been reprinted.

Sports

Lawn League: China Beats Portugal 111

Result: Nine to Six

Difficult Hope for Championship

The Chinese Tennis Association originally had enthusiastic hopes for the championship in the lawn tennis Group A league. Based on the past five games (winning 57 sets and losing 18 sets), there was reason to be optimistic. However, the turning point for competing with Japan for the top spot lay in yesterday's battle with Portugal. Although good news came that they won by nine to six, it seemed to be a notch below Japan's record. It may be very difficult for China 　to win this year's championship, and it may belong to Japan.

More than two hundred spectators watched quietly and applauded after enjoying it. The first, second, and third courts were the center of the crowd, and the fourth and fifth courts also had many appreciative spectators.

The Chinese lineup was different from before. The first group, Lin Baohua and Jiang Daozhang, were paired together, and the old couple reunited, giving the audience a lasting impression. The opposing team, Canafanloro and Leite, managed to regain the second set under difficult circumstances, which was no easy feat. In fact, Lin and Jiang could have won in three straight sets. The second group was represented by the up-and-coming stars Zheng Zhaojia and Yu Tianguang. They were effective in defeating the enemy in the first two sets, but they lacked stamina in the later stages and lost the last set. The third group, Feng Xikang and Guo Qida, tried their best to negotiate repeatedly, but they ultimately fell short and lost all three sets. The fourth group, Tu Kaiyuan and Qian Yaobin, were the most successful, winning all three sets in one go. Ran Deguang and Ma Anquan also had a clear advantage in the fifth group, winning two sets in a row before suddenly losing one set due to carelessness.

If the diplomatic situation does not improve, bonds may continue to fall.

There is a gradual motivation to sell tea from Fuliang. The output of green tea in the southeast of Fuliang is still good. Many people who transported Fuliang tea last year made a profit. This year, the local Xiuxiu tea merchants mistakenly expected the tea price to be higher than the old ones, and they all added their value and competed for purchase. They rushed to collect and transport it to the Shanghai market. The market was depressed and the price was unable to rise. Although the customers with goods in hand were eager to promote sales, the suffering merchants rejected them and did not enter, and it was shelved until now that they received the news that the Shanghai market had turned brisk and the low-priced goods were selling. The tea merchants took advantage of this good news to rush the stored goods to Wuzhuang for sale. Recently, the opening price in Wuzhuang has risen to 38 yuan to 40 yuan, and the sales have gradually gained motivation.

Tea Merchants Oppose Doubling Tea Tax 133

The Wan Finance Department of Huizhou Province had initially designated the tax rate on foreign box tea in the province as a special tax, changing the value to 20 out of 100, and sending staff to set up a bureau to specialize in collecting taxes. The tea merchants protested and requested the Ministry of Finance to reduce it. It was approved to handle it according to the case. However, each bureau collected taxes at 5 jiao and 5 fen per box, which was almost double the 2 jiao and 5 fen collected per box last year. Recently, various bureaus along the way have also intercepted box tea and forcibly collected taxes. The Xiuning Zhucun card bureau even committed a murder, causing public outrage. They telegraphed the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance to request a thorough investigation and stop. On one side, the Tunxi Tea Merchants Association sent letters to the trade associations in various counties to pay taxes at 2/1000 of the business income of Anhui Province from this month. The doubling of the harsh taxes of each bureau is resolutely opposed.

Free Talk

Man Is the Spirit of All Things 135

Words of the old man Ma Xiangbo, recorded by Fuji

I have a firm belief in religion, and I have a special interest in science. Looking up at the universe, I admire the greatness of the Creator. We human beings are uniquely endowed by nature, and we become the spirit of all things. Human beings can study all things, but all things cannot study human beings. I often imagine that the universe is so big, and the sun is in the middle of it. Human beings on earth seem big enough. But how big is the sun after all? Does the sun know itself? When I think of this, I point to the sun and laugh at it for a while.

(O Sun! O Sun!

I recognize you, but you don't recognize me.

Not only do I recognize you,

I also recognize myself.)

Only humans can recognize themselves, so humans are the spirit of all things. Man is the spirit of all things, man can recognize himself, so man can distinguish between good and evil. Some people say, (Good and evil are indefinite, they are created by habit.) I think otherwise, I have evidence to prove it.

When children see a sugar peddler, their mouths are dripping with saliva, but they don't dare to reach out and take it if they don't have money in their pockets. When the father takes out money to buy it, the sugar is in the child's hand, and whoever tries to snatch his sugar, he will cry. Children are human, children have souls, children know their place, children can recognize themselves.

On the other hand, Zhang San's dog is hungry and sees Li Si's things, so he snatches them to eat. Where do animals have Zhang San Li Si's division? Here we can see the difference between humans and animals, which is also a powerful proof that humans have souls.

The Suffering of Overseas Chinese in Japan 136

-- Gu Dai

I have a relative living with me who is engaged in the flower and tree business in Japan. He recently returned to his ancestral home in Wenzhou from Japan on the President Wilson. He passed through Shanghai and came to my residence to talk about old times. He also described what he had heard and seen in Japan since the September 18th Incident. In the long summer, I have plenty of time to retell it.

The Japanese have always had a mantra: "Chinese people are not as good as dogs." Therefore, Chinese people in Japan follow the instruction of eating more and speaking less. Because speaking more can lead to humiliation. Since the September 18th Incident, the Japanese have become more arbitrary, even regarding the Chinese as nothing. And they have even gone further and chanted "White people are not to be feared." When the Pan case first occurred, the Japanese were terrified of the intervention of the League of Nations. Therefore, there were often complaints in the newspapers about the recklessness of the army. Later, they saw that the so-called League of Nations was singing its empty city plan, and the Chinese government was still wholeheartedly begging for pity from the League of Nations. Everything was seen through by the Japanese, so they united from top to bottom and boldly went ahead. After occupying Liaoning and Jilin, they invaded Heilongjiang in the north. Their domestic newspapers were full of victory records. The Japanese were very happy, and the Chinese were even more despised. However, although the news of victory kept coming, reinforcements continued to be sent. There were also rumors in the market that so many people were transported back from North Manchuria who had died in battle. Later, it was learned that General Ma had annihilated the Japanese army that had occupied the two provinces of Liaoning and Jilin without bloodshed at the Nenjiang Bridge. Therefore, overseas Chinese in Japan seemed to be suspected of being spies for the Black Army. After the Black War stopped, the Shanghai Incident suddenly occurred. The news of the victory of the Japanese army was repeatedly transmitted to Tokyo. However, one week later, the Japanese had not taken a single step into Zhabei, and the conscription of reinforcements and the transportation of military equipment had not ceased. The commanders were changed frequently. Two weeks later, the dead and wounded were still being transported back. Due to the descriptions of the Nineteenth Route Army's divine power by the wounded, the overseas Chinese in Japan were suspected of being spies for the Nineteenth Route Army. After the retreat of the Nineteenth Route Army, the overseas Chinese returned to the status of subjugated slaves. When the Hongkou Park bombing occurred, the first message transmitted to the East said that the murderer was Korean. The overseas Chinese were relieved. However, many overseas Chinese who had dealings with Koreans were monitored because of suspicion. By this point, it was generally believed that all overseas Chinese in Japan were accomplices in the bombing. As the Northeastern Volunteer Army grew stronger and attacked from the east and west, the Japanese were quite embarrassed. The domestic economy became more and more difficult, and conscription was frequent. Young people joined the army, and all industries were stagnant. The overseas Chinese who depended on the Japanese for a living were regarded as bandits and were forced to return to China. On the day of departure, the port was heavily guarded. The baggage they carried was thoroughly searched. All the Japanese currency they carried was confiscated. A little resistance would be met with immediate beatings. The mantra "Chinese people are not as good as dogs" was known to every Japanese person.

The Thunderous Hand That Solves the Woes of Japanese Slaves 137

-- Lei Sheng

A certain gentleman, hiding his name, is from the South China Sea. Seven or eight years ago, he studied at Waseda University in Japan. He fell ill and was transferred to the hospital. The nurse, Ms. Yoshida, served him diligently. The gentleman was a handsome young man, and Yoshida was also beautiful. They fell in love. After recovering from his illness, he asked someone to introduce them and made a lifelong promise. They both returned to China. The gentleman worked in Shanghai. A son was born and died young. Last winter, the violent sun invaded Shanghai. Japanese expatriates returned one after another. Yoshida said goodbye to the gentleman. The gentleman tried hard to keep her. Yoshida was also hesitant, but she had to leave because of the situation. The gentleman only felt personal feelings and forgot national hatred. He even wanted to secretly follow Yoshida. His younger brother was also in Shanghai. When he heard about it, he urgently summoned his brother to a separate room and kept him there, while Yoshida left. He falsely said that the grandmother was critically ill in the hometown and the brother had already boarded the ship to return. He deeply knew that his brother was confused and could not be moved by words, so he used this thunderous hand. After Yoshida left, he gave his brother freedom and said to him: The ancients said that a resentful couple is an enemy. Now the brother's matter should be reversed and said that an enemy is a resentful couple. The brother is not afraid of ruining his reputation, but does he not care about his conscience? The gentleman knew that there was nothing he could do, so he thanked his brother and said, I was temporarily confused. Without the deep love of the brother, I would not be able to save myself. I said that in the past there were those who were caught in the beauty trap and humiliated the country, called the alliance under the bed. Although the gentleman's personal affairs are also visible to the danger of love, it is enough to warn later generations.

Idle Talk from the Red Chamber 138

— Cheng Junsong

Jia Baoyu said, "(Women are made of water, men are made of mud)." These two sentences are really not wrong. Mud will dissolve once it enters water. When men encounter women, how can they not be dissolved?

To compare important figures of the National Government to characters in "Dream of the Red Chamber": Lin Zichao is comparable to the virtuous and respected Old Lady Shi; Chiang Kai-shek is comparable to the shrewd and capable Wang Xifeng; Wu Zhihui is comparable to the dull-witted Granny Liu; Yu Youren is comparable to the stern and selfless Jiao Da (Apologies to Mr. Yu; be careful not to eat horse manure). Wang Jingwei is comparable to the intelligent and perceptive Baochai; Hu Hanmin is comparable to the sickly and melancholy Daiyu. Only this affectionate Baoyu cannot be compared to any contemporary talents. Alas, let's tentatively compare him to Zhang Xueliang.

When Jia Yucun was trying the Xue Pan manslaughter case, the advice given by the gatekeeper was indeed a "brocade bag" for officialdom, a secret to success in official life. If you are not afraid of power and influence, and disregard all considerations, insisting on doing things your way, then your rice bowl is guaranteed to be smashed immediately. Conversely, if you know how to flatter and ingratiate yourself, then you have the hope of being promoted and becoming wealthy.

Baoyu is, after all, a romantic soul. Even though he married Baochai, he still never forgot Daiyu in his heart, eventually becoming a monk and leaving. In contrast to today's youth who only know the pleasures of physical desire, he is not to be mentioned in the same breath.

Extreme prosperity is followed by decline, and the sun at its zenith must wane. This is a universal principle of natural evolution. When the Grand View Garden was at its peak, what grandeur, what glory, what extravagance! But by the time Baoyu became a monk, the Jia mother had passed away, and the property was confiscated, resulting in the family being broken and ruined. What desolation, what misery, what grief! I sincerely hope that the great and wealthy families of today maintain balance, avoid being too arrogant and extravagant, and constantly take this as a warning. Wang Xifeng's management of the household was considered responsible and willing to work hard. Ultimately, her energy was limited, and her attention could not be everywhere. Therefore, the embezzlement and corruption of her subordinates, and acts of petty theft, occurred frequently. Speaking of China's current politics, it is nothing less than a portrait of this.

Random Talks on Watermelons 139

— Shizi

Last summer, I wrote about watermelons, saying that the internal corruption of our country's internal affairs is like the inside of a watermelon being rotten, while strong neighbors surround us. Once they wield the knife and try to divide it, this internally rotten watermelon will not even be able to keep its rind. This was originally written from a temporary feeling. Unexpectedly, soon after, the September 18th Incident occurred, carving off a part of Northeast China from our entire China. Unfortunately, my words came true. How painful this is! Another year has passed, and it is summer again. Recalling this, sweat soaks my back. Therefore, I dare not recklessly make presumptions again. I will just write some random notes as embellishments for the hot summer.

When I was a child, I once got a black-skinned watermelon. I would cut off the top and use a spoon to scoop out the pulp, leaving the rind very thin. Then, with a sharp little knife, I would carve extremely fine patterns on the outer skin. I would also lightly apply colors to the carved patterns. I would light a short candle inside and hang it in front of the eaves, cooling off underneath. When the clear breeze came, the sweltering heat would disappear. Sometimes I would float it on the pond, and the swimming fish would compete to chase after it, which was quite interesting. In recent years, I have been bound by responsibilities and commitments, and have had no time to return to my hometown to escape the summer heat. Recalling the scenes of my childhood, I cannot help but be transported in spirit.

Farmers who plant watermelons can earn a profit of about one hundred yuan per acre in years of abundant harvest and high prices by picking them and transporting them to Shanghai for sale. Therefore, farmers in my hometown (east of Kunshan) must plant several acres of watermelons every year. If they can make a profit, then they can be free from worrying about food and clothing for a year. However, growing watermelons is quite speculative. It is not as stable as planting cotton or rice. This is because there are many kinds of animals in the watermelon fields. They come out in groups and can trample almost the entire ten acres of watermelon fields in an hour. Therefore, farmers take turns guarding them all night to prevent animals, and at the same time, they can also prevent thieves. When the watermelons are ripe, they are transported to Shanghai. If at that time, there are consecutive days of cloudy and rainy weather, and the "Red Emperor" (sun) hides its traces, and the watermelons cannot be stored for long, they can only be sold off at a low price, resulting in losses. When we buy watermelons, we smile broadly when the price is cheap, but we do not know that the farmers forget to eat and sleep, and the price they receive may not even be enough to pay the rent and repay the debts (the fertilizer required for watermelons is extremely expensive).

When we eat watermelons, we often discard the rind. In fact, if you remove the pulp from the watermelon rind and leave a two-tenths-inch thick layer of the rind, soak it in a little salt for about five or six hours, then pickle it in soy sauce (or even soybean paste) for about a day and night, then take it out and serve it with meals, it is fragrant, fresh, and tender, and its taste is excellent. It is especially suitable for those who avoid oily foods in the summer. This is also a way to make use of waste. Readers, why not give it a try?

Talk on Tortoiseshell Fan 140

— Yanzi

At this time when the days are long like years and the warm winds are like burning embers, the sea of fan exhibitions arises in response to the season. There are four companies, such as the Art Sea Backwater Society, the Lili Company, the Jiuyu Hall, and the Art Appreciation Society, all of which have attracted famous artists with superb calligraphy and painting skills. Only the Appreciation Society in Daqing Lane is organized by Qian Shoutie, a calligrapher, painter, and seal carver. Mr. Qian is heroic and good at making friends. Calligraphers and painters from all over the country are his acquaintances. Therefore, when he makes a call, all the mountains respond. The cooperative fan pieces are all carefully constructed works. Yesterday, I heard the news in the countryside and braved the summer heat to come to Shanghai. I went upstairs and looked all around. The walls were filled with exquisite works, making it a feast for the eyes. However, from my humble perspective, the red and white monthly roses jointly created by Bailong Shanren and Gong Zhan, Zhang Daqian's cattail cushion pine, Qian Shoutie, Chen Xiaodie, Lu Xiaoman, Fei Longding, and Sun Xueni's cooperative landscape paintings and calligraphy, Chen Xiaocui's figure paintings, Zhang Shimin and Wu Qingxia's cooperative plum blossoms and daffodils, Ye Weishen and Zheng Wuchang's cooperative shrimps and crabs, Shang Shengbo and Wang Shizi's cooperative flowers and birds, Ma Qizhou, Chen Xiaomei, Zhang Shanzi, and Xie Yucen's cooperative landscape paintings, Huang Binhong, Wang Zhongshan, Wu Yifeng, and Wang Shengyuan's landscape paintings, Xiong Songquan and Zhang Shanzi's lions and tigers, Shen Moxian's plum blossoms, Hong Shuan's flowers, birds, grass, and insects, Zhao Banpo's flowers, Wu Hufan, Peng Gongfu, He Tianjian, and Huang Suyun's landscape paintings, Ma Wanli's flowers and fruits, and Zhu Wenyun's orchids and bamboos are all famous for a time, without any distinction of rank. As for the newly emerging young people such as Hu Ruosi, Ma Daiyun, Liang Kaishi, and Wu Bin's meticulous imitation of ancient landscape paintings, the famous painter Huang Taixuan's running script paintings, Zhu Qi's flying white script, and Ren Xunshu and Qi Fanniu's running cursive script, all are rare masterpieces of the present time, making people feel as if they are on the road to Shanyin, and there is no time to take it all in. I returned home and recorded it by lamplight.

National Goods Factories Worth Introducing (6) 141

— He Gongxing

(9) Creosote Oil Factory

Creosote oil is made by mixing rosin and cresol (insecticide) in equal amounts, adding 0.03% caustic soda, and filtering twice.

The method of making cresol is to place coal tar in an iron pot and burn it intensely. It must be between 190 degrees and 270 degrees Celsius for the original material to change and become a type of cresol. Lysol, which is used in surgery, and naphthol, are both made from cresol. Creosote oil is a necessary product in summer. Its function is to kill insects and remove odors. In the past, most of the creosote oil came from Japan. Since the domestic creosote oil has been produced and sold, Japanese goods have been eliminated from the market. Currently, there are Yalin Creosote Oil Factory, whose products are the "Microscope" brand, and Asia Creosote Oil Factory, whose products are the "Double Knife" brand, in Shanghai. Others, such as the "Eagle" brand, are also well-known. The larger ones are packed in 40-gallon barrels. The market price is one yuan and three jiao per gallon, seven jiao for half a gallon, and four jiao for a quarter of a gallon.

Creosote oil factories often also make mothballs. The method is to use the above-mentioned naphthol, refine it with legal spirits, extract a kind of white block, and press it with a machine to make mothballs. Each pound sells for two jiao. This is a necessary item in wardrobes and bookshelves to prevent insect damage.

(10) Sun Umbrella Factory

Most of the sun umbrella manufacturers in Shanghai operate through division of labor. The poles, handles, ribs, and canopies are all made by the respective factories. The sun umbrella factory buys them and assembles them. However, Huali Shi mostly makes them themselves. Among them, making the ribs is more complicated. There are three or four factories in Shanghai that specialize in making umbrella ribs, such as the Sanxing Umbrella Rib Factory in Xiaoximen. The ribs are made of mild steel wire or steel wire, which is rolled, wheeled, and drilled by machine. The price is two yuan to two yuan per dozen, divided into black and white colors, and 3-foot and 2.8-inch sizes.

Most of the poles are made of foreign pine, each costing three to four cents. The quality of the handles varies. Some are made of wood, some are made of metal, and some are made of imitation treasures. In the past, they were all Japanese goods, but now they are mostly replaced by domestic goods. The most common wooden handles cost about nine jiao per dozen.

The materials used for the canopy also vary. Second- and third-class goods mostly use black factory cloth. A piece of 40 yards costs ten yuan. The canopies of first-class goods mostly use Western twill satin. Women's umbrellas use silk.

There are more than 30 sun umbrella factories in Shanghai, the larger ones being Huali Shi, Xin Dalu, Xin Datong, Minhua, Zhenhua, Meili, etc. Each factory produces 70 to 80 dozen or 20 to 30 dozen umbrellas per day. The price ranges from 11 yuan to more than 20 yuan per dozen. Women's silk umbrellas cost 50 to 60 yuan per dozen. The workers are paid by piece, such as two cents per umbrella for hemming and one cent per umbrella for attaching the top. After the umbrella top is attached, it must be steamed once to make the umbrella canopy flat and durable.

Local News

Northeast Customs Seized, We Will Reduce Foreign Debt Repayments 142

If necessary, all Japanese personnel in Liaoning customs will be dismissed. After the customs revenue of Dalian and the Northeast was seized by the puppet state instigated by the Japanese, we protested seriously to Japan twice. Recently, Chief Inspector of Customs, Mr. Moyler, decided to wait for the implementation of the blockade since Japan had not officially responded to the Dalian customs matter. Regarding the repayment of foreign debt, the government has reached an agreement with the countries concerned to reduce the amount of repayment. The transitional measures after the blockade will remain the same.

Reduced repayment of foreign debt. The seizure of customs in the Northeast has resulted in an average annual loss of more than 39 million yuan in national tax revenue. The repayment of foreign debt mortgaged with this tax revenue has been greatly affected. Japan, disregarding the sovereignty of our government and believing that we will be unable to cope, even promoted so-called mediation measures to cover up its crime of instigating the puppet state to seize the customs. This so-called mediation measure is not only difficult for our government to recognize, but also unacceptable to the countries concerned. However, the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs proposed a method of reducing the repayment amount in consultation with the countries concerned. As a result, the countries have fully agreed. However, the amount of reduction has not yet been determined, and the parties are still in consultation. Roughly, the amount will be calculated in proportion to the amount of tax revenue in the Northeast.

Liaoning Customs Blockade According to reliable sources, since the Chief Inspector of Customs proposed Mr. Anesaki to succeed Mr. Fukumoto as the Customs Officer of Dalian Customs and sought the consent of the Japanese, the Japanese have not officially replied. The news of rejection and consent previously reported by the Japanese propaganda agencies contained an intention. Chief Inspector of Customs Mr. Moyler has inquired to the Japanese Embassy twice and has already issued an ultimatum in the style of an ultimatum. He is now waiting for the reply. If the Japanese side still does not reply by the deadline, or if the reply is not satisfactory, we will resolutely and quickly blockade the customs of the Northeast. At the same time, a statement will be issued stating the responsibility. There are no problems with the post-blockade measures by the countries concerned. The countries have not recognized the puppet state, so the legitimate customs organization is ours. If the puppet state collects double taxes, it will throw a huge bomb at the business communities in Dalian, South Manchuria, and other parts of the Northeast. The Japanese government may not be able to predict this future fact.

Transitional Measures The tax authorities discussed the transitional measures before the blockade of the Northeast customs a few days ago, and decided to continue the existing general measures. It is said that the authorities expect that if the Japanese side does not reply and implements the blockade, it will not take long, so there is no need to take this matter in this shortest period.

Dismissal of Japanese Personnel Mr. Fukumoto, the Customs Officer of Dalian Customs, disobeyed orders and resigned. All Japanese customs officers in Dalian and other parts of the Northeast followed suit. Mr. Moyler was extremely angry about this and mentioned this matter in the statement announcing the dismissal of Mr. Fukumoto as Customs Officer. After consultation by the authorities, it has been decided that if the customs duties of the Northeast cannot be resolved satisfactorily, other Japanese customs officers will be dismissed except for those with special circumstances to prevent future troubles.

Japan Claims Difficulty The Japanese side instigated the puppet state to seize the customs duties, but did not expect that we still have this move. Because they made the mistake, they then felt that our attitude was tough. In recent days, they have delayed expressing their opinion on the dismissal of Mr. Fukumoto and the succession of Mr. Anesaki. According to people in diplomatic circles, this is a sign of fear. It is said that the Japanese side is in a dilemma at this time. If they agree to the succession of Mr. Anesaki, the new Customs Officer of Dalian, then the seizure of the customs in the Northeast clearly shows that the Japanese side admits to instigating it. Otherwise, if we implement the blockade, the puppet customs will not have any benefits, and the Japanese businesses in the Northeast, especially the city of Dalian and the South Manchuria Railway, will be severely hit.

Our Measures for the Northeast Postal Service 143

We will definitely blockade it if necessary.

A reporter from the Far East News Agency visited the Director-General of the Postal Administration yesterday to inquire about the attitude of our government towards the Northeast postal service. He was received by the Deputy Director, who gave the following responsible speech.

Current Status According to him, since the Mukden Incident, the Northeast postal service has been able to maintain itself until now thanks to the perseverance and courage of the responsible personnel. After the establishment of the puppet state, the Japanese instigated and used various methods to sabotage and threatened with alarming words, but they were ignored. Therefore, at present, all bureaus in the three provinces are operating as usual, with no changes from before the incident. Letters and remittances can be sent smoothly, and efforts are being made to shorten delivery times. Although the territory of the Northeast has changed, the postal service can still maintain its independent spirit in the midst of storms, which is due to the efforts of the employees and responsible persons in the three provinces.

Japanese Arrangements Seeing that repeated sabotage had failed to achieve their goals, the Japanese instigated the puppet state to actively arrange illegal seizure. According to reports received by the General Administration, the Japanese have already printed a large number of stamps for the puppet state and transported them to Liaoyang. They have also appointed a large number of puppet directors and puppet inspectors. It is said that the stamps will be issued on August 1st. Whether they will forcibly send personnel to seize the bureaus on August 1st has not yet been reported. However, the skilled postal workers summoned by the Japanese side are now being assigned to various important areas to wait for orders.

Government Determination Our government has long been aware of the Japanese instigation of the puppet state to seize our Northeast postal rights, so it has been prepared. The Ministry has made a decision on a concrete plan a few days ago. However, due to the matter involving diplomatic secrets, it is not convenient to announce it. In short, the Northeast postal service is an important lifeline of transportation and economy in the Northeast. We will never allow anyone to seize it. In any case, we will not hesitate to completely blockade the Northeast postal service if necessary.

Armed Japanese Soldiers Conduct Drills on Xiangyin Road 144

They were carried in armored vehicles and carried maps

The Takeover Committee negotiated on the basis of reason and stopped them

On the 14th and 15th, more than 30 armed Japanese soldiers in the jurisdiction of the 2nd Branch of the 7th District of the Public Security Bureau near Xiangyin Road took nine armored vehicles, carried maps, and conducted simulated shooting exercises, causing extreme panic among residents. Yao Benyuan, the head of the 2nd Branch of the 7th District, repeatedly negotiated to no avail, so he reported to the Public Security Bureau and the Takeover Committee at the same time, requesting that they negotiate on the basis of reason. Mr. Yao received an order from the Takeover Committee yesterday stating that the report had been received and that the committee had sent a special commissioner, Jin Gong, to negotiate with the Chief of Staff of the Japanese Military Headquarters, Mr. Samejima. According to the reply, they had met with Mr. Samejima and discussed the previous situation. It was said that the exercise was organized by a training area and involved only a few soldiers, and that there were no other intentions. They immediately negotiated on the basis of reason, and it was agreed that in the future, all exercises should be unarmed and the Public Security Bureau should be notified in advance. They should only depart after obtaining permission. Furthermore, carrying maps was not a normal practice and should be stopped to avoid misunderstandings. The Chief of Staff promised that there would be no objections. This order was for information.

He Yingqin returned to Nanjing last night 150

Talk about aviation construction and air defense equipment

It is only effective when the government and the people cooperate

According to the Central News Agency, Minister of Military Administration He Yingqin arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing on the 18th to attend the opening ceremony of Mr. Chen Yingshi's Memorial Hall. The reporter visited Mr. He at his residence yesterday and had the following conversation: (Question) Is the Minister aware of the details of the Japanese army's invasion of Rehe? (Answer) I have only seen reports of the Japanese army's invasion of Rehe in the newspapers and have not received any official reports. (Question) Has the government made sufficient preparations for national defense? (Answer) The government has of course made considerable preparations for national defense, but this can only be effective when the government and the people cooperate sincerely. The people of Shanghai deeply felt the necessity of aviation construction and air defense equipment during the January 28 Incident, but now that Japanese aircraft have flown to the Northeast to bomb, the people of Shanghai seem to have forgotten about aviation construction and air defense equipment. If every person in Shanghai contributes one yuan, several million yuan can be raised, and aviation construction and air defense equipment can be realized. Therefore, when we talk about national defense, we must realize that it is only effective when the people and the government cooperate sincerely, and it is not effective to merely chant high-sounding slogans. The establishment of the National Aviation Association is the beginning of the people and the government cooperating to expand national defense. There is another point about national defense that the people should pay attention to. In all the places passed through by the National Army to suppress the Communists, the Communists stationed there often communicate with the people and transfer all the supplies in advance. Not only are there no locals who are familiar with the area to guide the army, but there are also no food supplies for the army. Therefore, this is a difficult point in the work of suppressing the Communists. If the people lack complete defense projects against the invasion of foreigners, they should resist with the policy of "strengthening the walls and clearing the fields." However, the people not only do not do this, but some even willingly become traitors and seek glory by betraying the country. These people are the common enemy of the people. (Question) Where will the Shanghai Arsenal be moved? (Answer) Shanghai is not suitable for setting up an arsenal, so it has been decided to move it to another place, but the address has not yet been determined. (Question) What is the progress of the Communist suppression recently? (Answer) The Red bandits in the provinces are all fleeing east and west, and our army is deploying a encirclement to try to clear them. Therefore, there has been no major contact on the front line recently. (Question) When will the Minister return to Nanjing? (Answer) I am scheduled to return to Nanjing by night train tonight (that is, last night). (Question) Will you go to Jiangxi after returning to Nanjing? (Answer) I will stay in Nanjing for the time being. If necessary, I will go to Jiangxi again, because there is a special round trip steamer, which is very convenient.

Feng Cunren Pharmacy Reopens Today 153

Three Settlement Terms

The labor dispute at Feng Cunren Pharmacy on Sanma Road has been successfully resolved through the mediation of Du Yuesheng. All employees fully resumed work yesterday. Details are as follows:

Du's Mediation: After the Feng Cunren Pharmacy employees declared a strike, both labor and management insisted on their positions, leading to a serious stalemate that lasted for half a month. Du Yuesheng, along with Mr. Chen Junyi, Chen Cunren, and Lin Meiyan, recognizing that prolonged confrontation during the hot summer would inevitably endanger patients' lives, accepted the invitation of both parties to mediate in a private capacity. They convened representatives from the labor side (Zhao Zhenhui, Yuan Pinzhang, Feng Xingkang) and the Feng Cunren Pharmacy small group (Ye Yazhang, Fang Qinghe), as well as representatives from the management side (Feng Mengling, Feng Ziyi), to discuss a resolution. A decision was made on three settlement terms, to which both parties agreed. After the labor representatives sought the opinions of the employees, they also found the terms satisfactory, and the dispute was resolved.

Settlement Terms: The three settlement terms agreed upon the day before yesterday are as follows: (1) One month's worth of the year-end bonus under the name of Feng Cunren's main store will be paid first. The remainder will be settled after the accounts are audited and surplus funds are available. Bonuses under the name of Jia Guang Raw Drug Store will be issued as usual. (2) The substitute worker system will be implemented according to the conditions. (3) The management will provide 570 yuan for the workers' food and lodging expenses during the strike period (calculated at 30 yuan per day).

Reopening Today: Feng Cunren Pharmacy suffered significant losses due to the strike and business suspension. Now that the dispute has been resolved and all employees returned to work yesterday, the management has decided to resume regular business operations starting today.

The Causes and Consequences of the Dafeng Labor Dispute 155

Regarding the unresolved issues of the Dafeng labor dispute, the responsible members of the Chinese General United Association stated yesterday that the Dafeng Factory joined the association as a basic member two years ago. In January of this year, due to the war, the workers were dismissed and their wages were paid off. The workers were laid off. After March 1st, as local order gradually recovered, the factory reopened. Under austerity policies, 109 workers were laid off, each receiving a severance pay of 30 yuan, which they all received.

Page 14

Not long after, the laid-off workers went to the factory to demand work, but the factory refused.

On March 31st, the Social Affairs Bureau convened a mediation, and both parties reached an agreement, allowing the laid-off workers who had already received severance pay to temporarily sever ties with the factory. When the factory's business recovers to its original state in the future, the old workers will be given priority for employment. On May 5th, after the signing of the Sino-Japanese ceasefire agreement, the laid-off workers came to Shanghai one after another to demand entry into the factory. Thus, the point of contention between the two parties focused on whether the business had recovered to its original state. During this period of dispute, the workers once rushed into the workshop, and the management closed the factory twice to prevent the workers from invading and occupying the factory and destroying the machinery. The situation between the two parties was extremely tense. On June 11th, the Social Affairs Bureau mediated again and guaranteed the workers' actions, and the management reopened the factory. However, the root cause was not eliminated, and there was still no hope of reconciliation. On the 28th, the Social Affairs Bureau convened the last mediation, and both parties signed three agreements: (1) Maintain the entire first mediation, and the factory will give each worker 10 yuan for their travel expenses back home. (2) The factory shall, within the possible scope, consider restoring work. (3) If they voluntarily sever ties with the factory, each person will be given a subsidy of 80 yuan. Unexpectedly, although the labor side signed this agreement, they were not satisfied. On July 14th and 15th, they went on strike and obstructed work. The Public Safety Bureau took strict measures to arrest 15 workers and send them to court for processing. The union also announced the end of the strike on the 19th of this month. This is the general situation of the Dafeng labor dispute. It was finally stated that the restoration of work was impossible due to the situation. First, Dafeng's production capacity was greatly reduced due to the war. Second, according to the spirit of the original text of the second mediation, it was originally possible to employ within the possible scope. Now that the labor side has launched the former and adopted a forceful solution, an impossible situation has been created within the possible scope, which is very regrettable.

Letters and telegrams are ignored, while the International Telecommunications Bureau, which has the highest income, is exempt from the centralization order. There is widespread discontent. This is the third thing we ask you to correct. Moreover, we cannot help but speak out. Our country's telecommunications business has reached a critical juncture. If we do not quickly plan for rectification, bankruptcy will be imminent. Now that Director Zhong is back in charge of Electric Affairs, we secretly hope for a revival. We hope that you will carefully consider our situation, quickly and effectively merge wired and wireless communications to eliminate disputes and reduce expenses, thoroughly reform the bad system to clear accumulated problems, and allocate funds to repair the trunk lines of various provinces to facilitate communication. Our association, representing more than 20,000 employees, respectfully requests and impatiently awaits orders. Electric Affairs Public Welfare Association of the Ministry of Communications."

(3) Liu Taojun suggested (A) Start investigating the existing and destroyed houses in the disaster area, draw a map of what is existing and what is destroyed, and report to the meeting. It was resolved to be handled by the investigation team. (B) Investigate the currently restored shops. It was resolved to be the same as above. (C) Encourage the currently restored shops to come to the association for registration. It was resolved to be temporarily retained. (D) Advertise to solicit shop owners who have not restored their businesses but want to restore them to come to the association for registration so that the association can help them restore their businesses within its capabilities.
